<font color="#000066" size="2" face="Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><b>Helpful Quick Links</b></font><br>
<strong>Useful calculators and converters</strong><br>
Here's to a productive new year online: a quick list of simple yet practical links. From how to decide if it pays to refinance to how much you should tip to how to find the next full moon, there's something for everyone. Enjoy!
<br><br>
<strong>Computers:</strong>
<ul>

</ul>

</ul>

Sending this from PyMailCGI.  The message goes from the web
browser client, to the HTTP web server (running locally on 
the same machine), to the Python CGI script, and finally to 
the SMTP email server at comcast.net before being delivered 
to earthlink.net.  When later fetched in PyMailCGI again, 
it goes from the POP email server at earthlink, to the CGI 
script, and back to the web browser client.  The HTTP server
and CGI scripts are extra layers not present when using the 
PyMailGUI client program.

--Mark Lutz  (http://www.rmi.net/~lutz)

<H1>Python activities calendar</H1>
<HR>

<P>
Here is what my Python commitments calendar looked like
the last time I changed this page.  Most of these entries
are sessions of my <A HREF="mytrain.html">Python training</A> 
class.  Entries marked as "(public)" are open to individual 
enrollment.  Others are normally private classes.  I keep this
list reasonably up to date, but please contact me by email 
(<A HREF="mailto:lutz@rmi.net">lutz@rmi.net</A>) or phone 
(303-772-3919) to verify current availability.
</P>
<HR>
<BR>
